Joel Hirsch offered marriage and respectability, hoping one day to earn her love, if not the passion she had felt for a man whose memory still haunted them both. With Joel, Caroline built a new life, determined to bury the past--until her daughter E</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText17987242006268328051">Caroline fled wartime Europe with a shattered life and a devastating secret. Pregnant and unwed, she came to America in 1939. Joel Hirsch offered marriage and respectability, hoping one day to earn her love, if not the passion she had felt for a man whose memory still haunted them both. With Joel, Caroline built a new life, determined to bury the past--until her daughter Eve brought Caroline's carefully crafted world crashing down again, driven by a rage to learn the truth.</span>

<div itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope="" itemprop="reviews" class="review" id="review_369328365">
  <link href="http://www.goodreads.com/review/show/369328365" itemprop="url" />
  <a href="/user/show/5624045-norma-huss" class="left imgcol" title="Norma Huss"><img src="http://d.gr-assets.com/users/1442600771p2/5624045.jpg" alt="Norma Huss" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a href="/review/show/369328365?book_show_action=true" itemprop="publishDate" class="reviewDate createdAt right">Jul 23, 2012</a>

      <a href="/user/show/5624045-norma-huss" class="user" title="Norma Huss">Norma Huss</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars"><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="really liked it">really liked it</span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="really liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="really liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="really liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="really liked it"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText"> · </span>
          <a href="/book/show/880386.Legacy_of_Silence" title="Paperback 9780440226406" class="lightGreyText">review of another edition</a>


        


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a href="/review/list/5624045-norma-huss?shelf=saga" class="actionLinkLite">saga</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span style="" class="readable" id="reviewTextContainer369328365">
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11586474554824934841">This is a book of generations - two actually, although, it seems almost like three generations. It begins in 1938 with a girl, half Jewish, in Germany. She and her adopted sister escape, but their parents don't. The girl, Caroline, arrives in America, pregnant and unwed. The story continues into the next generation with Caroline's daughters. As I read, I thought I understood the title, Legacy of Silence, but I didn't really - not until the end. </span>

          </span>
        </div>

<div itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope="" itemprop="reviews" class="review nosyndicate" id="review_66019148">
  <link href="http://www.goodreads.com/review/show/66019148" itemprop="url" />
  <a href="/user/show/1519970-pam" class="left imgcol" title="Pam"><img src="http://d.gr-assets.com/users/1298403411p2/1519970.jpg" alt="Pam" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a href="/review/show/66019148?book_show_action=true" itemprop="publishDate" class="reviewDate createdAt right">Aug 17, 2009</a>

      <a href="/user/show/1519970-pam" class="user" title="Pam">Pam</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars"><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was amazing">it was amazing</span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was amazing"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was amazing"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was amazing"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was amazing"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText"> · </span>
          <a href="/book/show/880386.Legacy_of_Silence" title="Paperback 9780440226406" class="lightGreyText">review of another edition</a>


        


    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span style="" class="readable" id="reviewTextContainer66019148">
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3031863137013118872">I have read most of Belva Plain's work and have never been disappointed. She writes historical fiction with great clarity and accuracy. This reminded me that we really need to find out for ourselves about our ancestors, because, even our parents can be misled by their experience and may not have the whole story, and to have bitterness towards an ancestor will only hurt us. Search and find the real story for yourself and then forgive and forget what you don't understand.</span>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer6597656277606294682"> Lore is an orphaned girl who is adopted by a rich family in Berlin. The family has a younger, biologial daughter, Caroline. Story takes place starting at the beginning of WWII. Caroline is beautiful and has fallen in love with boy from her neighborhood. The boy's father is big in the <br />Nazi party, but the boy does not hold the same political views. The parents can see what is coming in Germany and send the girls to Switzerland to stay with friends until they can get out of Germany.<br />They never come</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText6597656277606294682"> Lore is an orphaned girl who is adopted by a rich family in Berlin. The family has a younger, biologial daughter, Caroline. Story takes place starting at the beginning of WWII. Caroline is beautiful and has fallen in love with boy from her neighborhood. The boy's father is big in the <br />Nazi party, but the boy does not hold the same political views. The parents can see what is coming in Germany and send the girls to Switzerland to stay with friends until they can get out of Germany.<br />They never come to Switzerland, so the girls go to the U.S. Lore never seems as likeable as a character as Caroline. Lore is not attractive and does not speak English. She has to work hard to learn the language and take up her old profession of nursing. Caroline discovers she is pregnant and Lore tell her that the boyfriend has dumped her and joined the Nazi party. <br /> It seems like in the story that things come much easier to Caroline and Lore is just along as the "old maid aunt." Neither one are very happy in life. There are many twists to the story as it continues through 3 generations of this family. <br /></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer12920167381019800229">To be honest, this book was an absolute pain to get through.. at least for me. I found the pace to be incredibly slow, the conversations to be forced, the characters to be the same.. And, before chapter 18 in my book (probably the last twenty or so pages of the book), I was convinced that the book review I was reading was for a completely different book.   <span style="display:none" id="freeText12920167381019800229">To be honest, this book was an absolute pain to get through.. at least for me. I found the pace to be incredibly slow, the conversations to be forced, the characters to be the same.. And, before chapter 18 in my book (probably the last twenty or so pages of the book), I was convinced that the book review I was reading was for a completely different book. Heavens, I'm still convinced that it gives the book more dimension than the book actually has to begin with.<br /><br />Would I recommend this book to anyone? No. I can name tons of books that have much better plot development, that don't skim over things, and that are actually interesting and enjoyable to read. It's unfortunate, but this book just wasn't for me.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer8262780265458052841">Belva Plain is such an engaging writer- I loved her "Evergreen" which to me is a classic...she writes in a way that is so effortless to read- the kind of books with such engaging and interesting character you cant put them down! She makes her characters people you can identify with and you develop feelings for them and you cant wait to see what happens to them! I really enjoy her work....This book was even better in the end as it comes full circle and proving even in families people never really</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText8262780265458052841">Belva Plain is such an engaging writer- I loved her "Evergreen" which to me is a classic...she writes in a way that is so effortless to read- the kind of books with such engaging and interesting character you cant put them down! She makes her characters people you can identify with and you develop feelings for them and you cant wait to see what happens to them! I really enjoy her work....This book was even better in the end as it comes full circle and proving even in families people never really know eachother- and you never really know what motivates people or what they are truly thinking....thoroughly enjoyable!</span>
  <a onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;" href="#" data-text-id="8262780265458052841">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

      <a href="/user/show/2028167-jane-patterson" class="user" title="Jane Patterson">Jane Patterson</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars"><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="really liked it">really liked it</span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="really liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="really liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="really liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="really liked it"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText"> · </span>
          <a href="/book/show/880386.Legacy_of_Silence" title="Paperback 9780440226406" class="lightGreyText">review of another edition</a>


        


    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span style="" class="readable" id="reviewTextContainer276315419">
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2665404671093996006">This book was good down to the last page. It is about a mother, her first daughter and a 2nd daughter born 19 years later. It starts out in Europe around 1939 and ends in America about 1993. The lesson here is never assume something about someone because that assumption could be totally false and alter the way you live your life</span>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a href="/review/show/8466324?book_show_action=true" itemprop="publishDate" class="reviewDate createdAt right">Oct 30, 2007</a>

      <a href="/user/show/564223-kathy" class="user" title="Kathy">Kathy</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars"><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="liked it">liked it</span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="liked it"></span></span>

            Shelves:
              <a href="/review/list/564223-kathy?shelf=fiction-novels" class="actionLinkLite">fiction-novels</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span style="" class="readable" id="reviewTextContainer8466324">
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15038166003276213201"> This is the story of two sisters who escape from Nazi Germany in 1939. Their parents don't survive. Caroline is beautiful, and pregnant with a missing lover. Lore is adopted and not so attractive. They eventually immigrate to the US to begin new lives, but their past haunts them when a love interest comes between them.</span>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked &amp;&amp; exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&amp;name=' + shelf_name + '&amp;a=' + action + '&amp;authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('cOChKj5k+HMtfjQ6nzKIPP2dSJf92RMGAh3vdCgJ40UVNJ75zLbsiaGmQIHhU26OtGqLjrQEVKxoFOrm5JwVAA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

En stor Swanbåt ligger längst fram, men plötsligt faller den av. Skepparen är skjuten, mitt på öppet hav.\n\nThomas Andreasson, som befinner sig i publiken tillsammans med en gammal kollega från sjöpolisen, inser omedelbart allvaret. Med motorn på högsta varv styr de sin båt mot den stora kappseglaren där besättningen befinner sig i chock.\n\nOffret visar sig vara Oscar Juliander, framgångsrik seglare och vice ordförande i Kungliga Svenska Segelsällskapet. En känd och etablerad advokat som gärna har synts i medierna. Pressen på polisen att snabbt lösa fallet blir stor. Återigen har Nackapolisen fått ett sommarmord på halsen.\n\nThomas Andreasson, Margit Grankvist och de andra i teamet börjar kartlägga Julianders liv, och de får stiga in i överklassens salonger. Snart inser de att Julianders tjusiga fasad döljer otrohet, droger, fiffel och hotelser. Men vad har han egentligen gjort som fått någon att mörda honom på ett så utstuderat sätt?     <div class=" clearFloats bigBox" id="aboutAuthor"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/author/show/10209.Belva_Plain">About Belva Plain</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
      <a href="/author/show/10209.Belva_Plain"><img alt="10209" src="http://d.gr-assets.com/authors/1322448699p2/10209.jpg" class="right" /></a>
    <div class="readable">
      
<span id="freeTextContainer8203324962355438490">Belva Plain was a best-selling American author of mainstream women's fiction. Her first novel, <em>Evergreen</em> (1978) topped the New York Times bestseller list for 41 weeks and was made into a TV miniseries. At her death, there were over 30 million copies of her twenty-plus novels in print in 22 languages.<br /><br /></span>

    </div>
    <a href="/author/show/10209.Belva_Plain" class="actionLink moreLink">More about Belva Plain...</a>
<div class="clear"></div></div></div><div class="bigBoxBottom"></div></div>
